  834 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     73 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8418               | * We use a traditional Bresenham run-length approach.
  835 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     74 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8418               | * Run-slicing is possible, but the code is larger
  836 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     75 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8418               | * and the increased cost means it's only valuable
  837 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     76 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8418               | * for longer lines.  An optimal solution would switch
  838 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     77 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8418               | * approaches based on line length.

  847 |  2   FDRAW.LINE.s     86 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/8418               | * inclusive coordinates, means abs(x0-x1) > 254.

 1390 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     50 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * Calculate a circle, using Bresenham's algorithm.  The
 1391 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     51 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * results are placed into the rasterization buffers.
 1392 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     52 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | *
 1393 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     53 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * in_rad must be from 0 to 255.  The x/y center
 1394 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     54 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * coordinates must be on the screen, but the circle
 1395 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     55 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * can extend off the edge.
 1396 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     56 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | *
 1397 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     57 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * The computed values are stored in the rasterization
 1398 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     58 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * tables.  For an outline circle, we also plot the
 1399 |  3 FDRAW.CIRCLE.s     59 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/86BE               | * points immediately.

 2333 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    200 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/9300               | * RastFill unrolled loop.  At each step we store the current
 2334 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    201 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/9300               | * color value, XOR it to flip the bits if needed, and advance.
 2335 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    202 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/9300               | * The caller needs to set the appropriate initial value based

 2338 |  4 FDRAW.TABLES.s    205 | Comment     | 11 |         |    0 | 00/9300               | * We can use a 3-cycle "EOR dp" or a 2-cycle "EOR imm".  The
